| <span data-ttu-id="92ff2-462">Eingabe</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="92ff2-462">Entry</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="92ff2-463">Wert</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="92ff2-463">Value</span></span> |
